[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1106[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1108[0m[39m:  const uint8_t *last_src_pos = spos + len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1109[0m[39m:  buf = [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t *[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mwmem_alloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo->pool, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1111[0m[39m:  skip = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1112[0m[39m:  l = len;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1113[0m[39m:  [0m[1;35mwhile[0m[1;39m([0m[39ml > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1114[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m XXX Add expert info if spos >= last_src_pos?[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1115[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39mspos < last_src_pos && [0m[1;39m([0m[39mspos[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xff[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m[1;39m([0m[39mspos[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xff[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1116[0m[39m:      skip++;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1117[0m[39m:      l -= [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1118[0m[39m:      *[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdpos++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m0xff[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1119[0m[39m:      spos += [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1122[0m[39m:    *[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdpos++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m = *[0m[1;39m([0m[39mspos++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1123[0m[39m:    l--;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1124[0m[39m:  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1125[0m[39m:  option_subneg_tvb = [0m[1;35mtvb_new_child_real_data[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, buf, len-skip, len-skip[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1126[0m[39m:  [0m[1;35madd_new_data_source[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo, option_subneg_tvb, [0m[32m"Unpacked Telnet Option"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1127[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1128[0m[39m:  return option_subneg_tvb;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1129[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify and remove the premature free of the NAWS buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`hf_naws_data`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccurs during suboption parsing, and defer its deallocation until after the entire [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTelnet packet has been dissected. Specifically:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Locate the [0m[1;35mcall[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in `packet-telnet.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39minside `telnet_sub_option` or [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`telnet_command`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that invoke `wmem_free`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`wmem_simple_free` on `hf_naws_data` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mas [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mevidenced by the ASan log pointing to `wmem_simple_free` at line ~[0m[1;36m2099[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Remove or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconditionally bypass those calls to prevent reclaiming the NAWS buffer immediately [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mafter suboption handling.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Ensure the NAWS buffer remains valid through the subsequent text‐adding stage [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`telnet_add_text`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `dissect_telnet` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m2274[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, at the very beginning of the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction, reset all NAWS‐related globals to a known clean state:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;`[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `hf_telnet_line = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;`[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `hf_telnet_width = hf_telnet_height = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;`[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `hf_naws_data = NULL;`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. After the main parsing loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjust before the `return` in `dissect_telnet`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madd logic to free the NAWS buffer exactly once if it was allocated:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhf_telnet_naws_subopt_set && hf_naws_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mwmem_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo->pool, hf_naws_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        hf_telnet_line = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        hf_naws_data = NULL;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      This ensures the buffer lives through all calls to `telnet_add_text` and is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly reclaimed when no longer needed.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Verify that `dissect_naws_subopt` still allocates the buffer on `pinfo->pool` as[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   hf_naws_data = [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mwmem_alloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo->pool, hf_telnet_width * [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhf_telnet_height[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This allocation will now persist until the deferred free in `dissect_telnet`.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. By moving the free to the end of the dissector:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We preserve existing parsing logic and the use of [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tvb_get_raw_bytes_as_stringz` in `telnet_add_text`.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We do not alter harness or test code.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We continue to use the simple wmem allocator for per‐packet lifetime buffers, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoiding glib or manual `malloc`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`free` conversions.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Update and run the existing test suite and fuzz target to confirm that:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The AddressSanitizer heap‐use‐after‐free error is resolved.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - There are no memory leaks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe buffer is freed exactly once per packet[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other dissector functionality is inadvertently broken.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Document the change with a short comment in `dissect_telnet` explaining why the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNAWS buffer free was deferred, referencing the heap‐use‐after‐free issue.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Deferring the free until after the entire packet parsing retains the lifetime of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe NAWS buffer across both suboption handling and text addition phases, [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminating the use‐after‐free.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Using the existing wmem allocator and its API [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`wmem_alloc`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`wmem_free`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserves Wireshark’s memory‐management conventions.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Resetting globals at the start of `dissect_telnet` avoids cross‐frame state [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleakage.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This fix does not modify any harness or fuzzing logic and maintains all existing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munit and integration tests.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
